<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***прикидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикидывать.html>прики́дывать</a> (7786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">прики́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prikíd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикидывать.html>прики́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to estimate, to make a rough calculation, to ballpark
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикидывать.html>прики́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уме́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikídyvatʹ</b> v umé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weigh up; (try to) figure out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикидывать.html>прики́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>веса́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikídyvatʹ</b> na vesáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weigh</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gauge, to size up, to weigh up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to try on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw in, to add</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикидываться.html>прики́дываться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikídyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуться.html>прики́нуться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikínutʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***прикидывающий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикидывающий.html>прики́дывающий</a> (7786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***прикинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a> (6254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикидывать.html>прики́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to estimate, to make a rough calculation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уме́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikínutʹ</b> v umé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weigh up; (try to) figure out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>веса́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikínutʹ</b> na vesáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weigh</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gauge, to size up, to weigh up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нули</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решить.html>реши́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">my tut <b>prikínuli</b> i rešíli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we've weighed it up and come to a decision</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to try on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw in, to add</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prikínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуться.html>прики́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикидываться.html>прики́дываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pretend to be, to feign, to act
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуться.html>прики́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больны́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikínutʹsja</b> bolʹným</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pretend to be ill, to feign illness</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикинуть.html>прики́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prikínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***прикипевший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикипевший.html>прикипе́вший</a> (28494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикипевший.html>прикипе́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikipévšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикипеть.html>прикипе́ть</a> (28494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kipétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***прикладывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a> (9847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кла́дывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put (next to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikládyvatʹ</b> časý k úxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a watch to one's ear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырьку́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikládyvatʹ</b> rúku k kozyrʹkú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put one's hand to the peak of one's cap, salute</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikládyvatʹ</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to sign, fix one's signature 2) take a hand (in), put one's hand, to have a finger in the pie</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to attach, to enclose, to join
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikládyvatʹ</b> pečátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attach a seal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:усилие.html>уси́лия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikládyvatʹ</b> usílija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to apply force</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>класть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">klastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***прикладываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикладываться.html>прикла́дываться</a> (21923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prikládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладываться.html>прикла́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikládyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приложиться.html>приложи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put oneself <i>(to)</i>, to press oneself <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладываться.html>прикла́дываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земле́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikládyvatʹsja</b> úxom k zemlé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put one's ear to the ground</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take aim</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kiss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладываться.html>прикла́дываться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prikládyvatʹsja k butýlke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hit the bottle, commune with the spirits, bend one's elbow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prikládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагать.html>прилага́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prilagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладной.html>прикладно́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikladnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приклад.html>прикла́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priklád</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***приключиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приключиться.html>приключи́ться</a> (13550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ключи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приключиться.html>приключи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priključítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приключа́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to happen, to occur</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***приковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приковать.html>прикова́ть</a> (10527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приковать.html>прикова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приковывать.html>прико́вывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to chain</li>
<li>to rivet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приковать.html>прикова́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikovátʹ</b> čʹjó-libo vnimánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to absorb/rivet/compel/arrest/engross somebody's attention</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикованный.html>прико́вано</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mojó vnimánije býlo prikóvano (k)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">my attention was riveted (on)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pin down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приковать.html>прикова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сту</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">strax <b>prikovál</b> jevó k méstu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">fear rooted him to the spot/ground</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикованный.html>прико́ванный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikóvannyj</b> k postéli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">bedridden</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикованный.html>прико́ванный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́слу</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikóvannyj</b> k kréslu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">confined to one's armchair</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикованный.html>прико́ванный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвалидный.html>инвали́дной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коляска.html>коля́ске</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikóvannyj</b> k invalídnoj koljáske</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">wheelchair-bound</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приковать.html>прикова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prikovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приковывать.html>прико́вывающий</a> (29031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приковывать.html>прико́вывающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikóvyvajuščij</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикол.html>прико́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikól</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> speech</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> not bad!</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикол.html>прико́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикол.html>прико́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикол.html>прико́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приколоть.html>прико́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> joke
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикол.html>прико́л</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>Где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:откопать.html>откопа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граммофон.html>граммофо́н</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vot éto <b>prikól</b>! Gde ty otkopál étot stáryj grammofón?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a joke! Where did you dig up that old record player?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> storage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прикол.html>прико́ле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stojátʹ na <b>prikóle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be laid up</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
